<script type="text/javascript">
var absoluteURL = "http://www.debenhams.com/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/";
var imageDirectoryPath = "/wcsstore/DebenhamsUKSite/";
var styleDirectoryPath = "images/colors/color3/";
var tmInitialised = false;

//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
//Description: Dojo does not handle the case where the parameters in the URL are delimeted by the "/" forward slash. Therefore, in order to
//             workaround the issue, all AJAX requests must be done using absolute URLs rather than relative.
//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
function getAbsoluteURL()
{
	if (absoluteURL != "") {
		var currentURL = document.URL;
		var currentProtocol = "";
	
		if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
			currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
		
		var savedProtocol = "";
		if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
			savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
		
		if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
			absoluteURL = currentProtocol + absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
	}
	
	return absoluteURL;
}
//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the shared image directory.
//Description: In order to get the image directory path in any javascript file, this function can be used.
//Returns: The path to reference images.
function getImageDirectoryPath()
{
	return imageDirectoryPath;
}
//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the directory containing color-dependant image files.
//Description: In order to get the directory containing color-dependant image files in any javascript file, this function can be used.
//Returns: The path to reference color-dependant image files.
function getStyleDirectoryPath()
{
	return styleDirectoryPath;
}
/**
 * Added as part of the defect 37682.
 *
 */
function validateEmail()
{		
	var eMail = dojo.byId("subscribe_form_email").value;
	
	if(eMail!=null && !MessageHelper.isValidEmail(eMail)){
		MessageHelper.formErrorHandleClient("subscribe_form_email", MessageHelper.messages["ERROR_INVALIDEMAILFORMAT"]);	
		return false;	
	}
}

/**
 * Added as part of Checkout redesign.
 *
 */
function validateStayInTouch()
{	
	var stayInTouch = dojo.byId("stayInTouch").checked;
	if(stayInTouch == true){		
		clickDeliveryPayContainer2('Staying in touch','Receive Debs Plc comms:Yes');
	} else {		
		clickDeliveryPayContainer2('Staying in touch','Receive Debs Plc comms:No');
	}	
}

var geocoder  ;

function initialize()
{
    geocoder  = new google.maps.Geocoder();
}
function locationDetails(viewAll)
{
	var address;	
	if(document.getElementById("TownOrPostcodeField") !=null){
    	address = document.getElementById("TownOrPostcodeField").value;    	 
    }
    if((address != null && address != "") && !ShipmodeSelectionExtJS.validateZipCode('TownOrPostcodeField')){
    		document.getElementById("invalidZipCode").style.display = 'block';
	        document.getElementById("invalidZipCode").className = 'message error exclamation-mark';
	        document.getElementById("invalidZipCode").innerHTML = 'Invalid town or postcode';
	        if(document.getElementById("emptyZipCode")	!= "" ){	        
	        	document.getElementById("emptyZipCode").innerHTML = "";
	        	document.getElementById("emptyZipCode").className = '';
	        }
	        var previousResult = document.getElementById("StoreListResults");
	        if(previousResult != null || previousResult != "")
	       	previousResult.innerHTML = "";
	        var previousStoreDetails = document.getElementById("StoreDetails");
	        if(previousStoreDetails != null || previousResult != ""){
	        	previousStoreDetails.innerHTML = "";
	        	document.getElementById("DeliveryOptionConfirmRefreshArea").innerHTML = "";
	        }		
	}else{      
    var flgAddressUnknown = true; 
    var geoNodeForSearch = "";
    var url = "";
    var langId="-1";
    var storeId="10701";
    var catalogId="10001";
    
 
    if(geocoder == null)
    {
        geocoder  = new google.maps.Geocoder();
    }   
    if(viewAll == true || flgAddressUnknown == true)
    {
        if(document.getElementById("countryOfLogIn") !=null)
        	geoNodeForSearch = document.getElementById("countryOfLogIn").value;
    }
    
    if(address != null && address != ""){
     //making the DeliveryOptionConfirmRefreshArea div empty if the user tries search after selecting the store.
     if(document.getElementById("DeliveryOptionConfirmRefreshArea")!=null)
		document.getElementById("DeliveryOptionConfirmRefreshArea").innerHTML = "";
     
     var countryCode = document.getElementById("CFSsite").value;
     var addressCountry = address + " " + countryCode;
     geocoder.geocode( { 'address': addressCountry}, function(results, status) {        
    if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
        var latitude = results[0].geometry.location.lat();
        var longitude = results[0].geometry.location.lng();
                
        url="SelectedStoreListView?address="+address+"&langId="+langId+"&storeId="+storeId+"&catalogId="+catalogId+"&latitude="+latitude+"&longitude="+longitude+"&fromCheckout=true&geoNodeId="+geoNodeForSearch;
    
        CommonControllersDeclarationJS.setControllerURL("DebStoreListDisplay_Controller",url);
        wc.render.updateContext("DebStoreListDisplay_Context");
        
                          
    } else {                
                document.getElementById("NoResultFound").style.display = 'block';
                var previousResult = document.getElementById("StoreListResults");
	           	if(previousResult != null || previousResult != "")
	           	previousResult.innerHTML = "";
	           	var previousStoreDetails = document.getElementById("StoreDetails");
	           	if(previousStoreDetails != null || previousResult != ""){
	           		previousStoreDetails.innerHTML = "";
	           		document.getElementById("DeliveryOptionConfirmRefreshArea").innerHTML = "";
	           	}
	           	if(document.getElementById("invalidZipCode") != ""){
	           			document.getElementById("invalidZipCode").innerHTML = "";
	           			document.getElementById("invalidZipCode").className = '';
	           	}
	           	if(document.getElementById("emptyZipCode")	!= "" ){	        
		        	document.getElementById("emptyZipCode").innerHTML = "";
		        	document.getElementById("emptyZipCode").className = '';
		        }
           }
     });
     }
     else
     {
        if(geoNodeForSearch!=null && geoNodeForSearch != "" )
        {
           if(viewAll == 'deliveryStoreLocator'){
           	if(ShipmodeSelectionExtJS.validateZipCode('TownOrPostcodeField')){
		           url="SelectedStoreListView?langId="+langId+"&storeId="+storeId+"&catalogId="+catalogId+"&geoNodeId="+geoNodeForSearch+"&fromCheckout=true";
		           CommonControllersDeclarationJS.setControllerURL("DebStoreListDisplay_Controller",url);           
		           wc.render.updateContext("DebStoreListDisplay_Context");
	           }else{
	           		document.getElementById("emptyZipCode").style.display = 'block';
	           		document.getElementById("emptyZipCode").className = 'message error exclamation-mark';
	           		document.getElementById("emptyZipCode").innerHTML = 'Please enter the town or postcode';
	           		if(document.getElementById("invalidZipCode") != ""){
	           			document.getElementById("invalidZipCode").innerHTML = "";
	           			document.getElementById("invalidZipCode").className = '';
	           		}
	           		var previousResult = document.getElementById("StoreListResults");
	           		if(previousResult != null || previousResult != "")
	           			previousResult.innerHTML = "";
	           		var previousStoreDetails = document.getElementById("StoreDetails");
	           		if(previousStoreDetails != null || previousResult != ""){
	           			previousStoreDetails.innerHTML = "";
	           			document.getElementById("DeliveryOptionConfirmRefreshArea").innerHTML = "";
	           		}
	           }
           } else{
           		url="SelectedStoreListView?langId="+langId+"&storeId="+storeId+"&catalogId="+catalogId+"&geoNodeId="+geoNodeForSearch+"&fromCheckout=true";
	       		CommonControllersDeclarationJS.setControllerURL("DebStoreListDisplay_Controller",url);           
	           	wc.render.updateContext("DebStoreListDisplay_Context");
           }
        }
     }
	}
}
</script>

		console.log('Deleting cookie ' + cookieName);
		document.cookie = cookieName + '=expireNow;path=/;expires=Thu, 01-Jan-1970 00:00:01 GMT';
	};
	function deleteCookies() {
		// delete cookies for CSR
		var storeId = '10701';
		deleteCookie('Debs-' + storeId + '-CSR');
	};
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	/**
	 * function to delete cookie (via expire)
	 */
	function deleteCookie(cookieName) {
		document.cookie = cookieName + '=expireNow;path=/;expires=Thu, 01-Jan-1970 00:00:01 GMT';
	};
	function deleteAllCookies() {
		// delete cookies for CSR
		var storeId = '10701';
		if (typeof getCookie('Debs-' + storeId + '-runAsUserId') != 'undefined') {
			var runAsUserId = getCookie('Debs-' + storeId + '-runAsUserId');
			var node = dojo.byId('CSREnactmentHeader');
			if (node) {
				var divHtml = node.innerHTML;
				node.innerHTML = divHtml.replace(runAsUserId, "runAsUserIdValue");
			}
			deleteCookie('Debs-' + storeId + '-runAsUserId');
			
		}
		deleteCookie('Debs-' + storeId + '-CSR');
	};
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var $Deb={};
$Deb.oneGetParam=function(url,key){var urlparts=url.split('?');if(urlparts[1]){var kvps=urlparts[1].split('&');if(kvps.length)for(var i=0;i<kvps.length;i++)if(kvps[i].indexOf(key+'=')!=-1)return kvps[i].replace(key+'=','');}return false;};
$Deb.setCookie=function(a,c,b,d,f,g){var e=new Date;e.setTime(e.getTime());if(b)b=b*1E3*60*60*24;e=new Date(e.getTime()+b);document.cookie=a+"="+escape(c)+(b?";expires="+e.toGMTString():"")+(d?";path="+d:"")+(f?";domain="+f:"")+(g?";secure":"")};
$Deb.getCookie=function(a){var c="",b=" "+document.cookie+";",d=" "+a+"=";a=b.indexOf(d);if(a!=-1){a+=d.length;c=b.indexOf(";",a);c=unescape(b.substring(a,c))}return c};

/* MSITE REDIR */
(function(){
	var ua=navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
	function isiPhoneOrTouch(){return (ua.indexOf("iphone;")>=0||ua.indexOf("ipod;")>=0)};
	function isSmallDevice() {if (screen.width >= 1000){return false;}var cwidth = screen.width;var cheight = screen.height;if (ua.indexOf("android") < 0){var dpr = ((window.devicePixelRatio === undefined) ? 1 : window.devicePixelRatio);cwidth = (cwidth / dpr);cheight = (cheight / dpr);}return ((Math.min(cheight,cwidth) < 480) || (Math.max(cheight,cwidth) < 800));}
	function isAndroidMobile(){return ((ua.indexOf("android")>=0) && (ua.indexOf('mobile') >= 0));};
    function isMacintosh() {return (ua.indexOf("macintosh") >= 0); }
    function isTouchEnabled() {return ('ontouchstart' in window || 'onmsgesturechange' in window);}

	var cookieName,cookieValue,expires=365,path=null,domain=null,secure=null;

	if(ua.indexOf("ipad;")>=0){
		return false;
		var popupShownCookie='iPadApp';
		var popupShown=$Deb.getCookie(popupShownCookie);
		var path='/',domain=null,secure=null;
		if(!popupShown){
			var ineligibleDateCookie='ineligibleDate';
			var ineligibleDate=$Deb.getCookie(ineligibleDateCookie);
			var now=new Date();
			var todaysDate=now.getDate()+'-'+(now.getMonth()+1)+'-'+now.getFullYear();
			if(ineligibleDate){
				if(ineligibleDate!==todaysDate){
					if(window.location.search.toLowerCase().indexOf('cmp=emc')>=0){
						$Deb.setCookie(ineligibleDateCookie,todaysDate,30,path,domain,secure);
					}else{
						$Deb.setCookie(popupShownCookie,1,365,path,domain,secure);
						$Deb.setCookie(ineligibleDateCookie,1,-1,path,domain,secure);
						if(confirm("Have you downloaded our new iPad app?\nWe think it's a much better way of viewing Debenhams on your iPad and it is completely FREE")){
							window.location.href='itms://itunes.apple.com/gb/app/debenhams-for-ipad/id470540241?mt=8';
						}
					}
				}
			}else{
				setCookie(ineligibleDateCookie,todaysDate,30,path,domain,secure);
			}
		}
	}

	cookieName='MBak2Full';
	cookieValue=$Deb.getCookie(cookieName);
	if($Deb.oneGetParam(window.location.toString(),'m-back2full')){
		$Deb.setCookie(cookieName,'true',null,path,domain,secure);
		cookieValue='true';
	}
	if(cookieValue!='true'){if(!isMacintosh() && isTouchEnabled() && (isiPhoneOrTouch() || isAndroidMobile() ||isSmallDevice())&&(parent.location.protocol=="http:")){
		/* optimized MSite redirect */
		var a = document.createElement('a');
		a.href = document.location.href.replace("iwwisb01.","www.").replace('www.debenhams.com','m.debenhams.com');

        //If we are already on the domain, don't redirect
        if (a.href === document.location.href){return false;}
        if(document.referrer){a.search+=(a.search[0]=="?"?"&":"?")+"m-referrer="+encodeURIComponent(document.referrer);}
		window.location.replace(a.href.substring(0,2000));
	}}
})();

<script type="text/javascript">

var lazyLoadTopNavImage = function() {
	if(!$(this).hasClass('lazyloaded'))
	{
		var $imgEl = $(this).find('img'); 

		if($imgEl.length > 0)
		{	
			var dataSrc = $imgEl.attr('data-src');
			$imgEl.attr('src', dataSrc);
			$(this).addClass('lazyloaded'); 
		}
	}
}

if($('.main-logo').css('display') != "none"){
	eventType="mouseenter";
} else {
	eventType="click";
}
$('#navMenuHolder ul.menu-l1-li-hld > li.menu-l1-li').bind(eventType, lazyLoadTopNavImage);

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var $Deb = $Deb || {};

/* If the page is a T-CAT */
$Deb.isTCAT=$("#WC_Shop_TopCategory_TCAT_Body").length;
/* If the page is a PSP */
$Deb.isPSP=$("#WC_Shop_ProductSelectionPage_PSP_Body").length;
/* If the page is a PDP */
$Deb.isPDP = $('#WC_Shop_ProductDisplay_Body').length;

/* Failed Search */
if ( $Deb.isPSP && $('#products_found').text().indexOf(' no product') > -1 ){
    $("#body_content_ProductSelectionPage").addClass("failed-search-enabled");
    $.ajax({ url: '/wcsstore/DebenhamsUKSite/js/Deb.FS.js', dataType: 'script', cache: true});
}


/* Set Vortal Name */
$Deb.vortalName=null;
$Deb.setVortalName=function(){
	var c=$('#breadcrumb_cat .breadcrumb').map( function( i, el ){ return $(el).text(); });
	if(c[1]){$Deb.vortalName=$.trim(c[1]);}
};



/* Install SBCodeRules, auto-convert promoCode field to uppercase */
$(document).ready(function() {
	if($('#promoCode').length>0 && $('#WC_Shop_OrderItemDisplay_Body').length>0) {
		var s=document.createElement('script');
		s.type='text/javascript';
		s.async=true;
		s.src='/wcsstore/DebenhamsUKSite/js/Deb.SBCodeRules.js';
		var s1=document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
		s1.parentNode.insertBefore(s,s1);

		$("#promoCode").live('keyup',function(){
			$(this).val($(this).val().toUpperCase());
		});
	}
});


/** Last Track module */
(function(container, $, window) {
	function createModule() {
		var cookieName = 'debUserEngage';
			
		function runMonitor() {
			var currCookie = window.$Deb.getCookie(cookieName);
			if(currCookie) {
				var cookieDates = currCookie.split("|");
				if(cookieDates[0] != getCurrentDate()) {
					updateCookie([getCurrentDate(), cookieDates[0]]);
				}
			} else {
				updateCookie([getCurrentDate(), '']);
			}
		}
		
		function updateCookie(cookieData) {
			window.$Deb.setCookie(cookieName, cookieData.join("|"), 365, '/', null);
		}
		
		function getCurrentDate() {
			var d = new Date();
			return d.getDate() + '-' + d.getMonth() + '-' + d.getFullYear();
		}
		
		return {
			init: runMonitor
		};
	}
	container.lastTrack = createModule();
})($Deb, jQuery, window);

$Deb.lastTrack.init();

<script type="text/javascript" src="/wcsstore/DebenhamsUKSite/data/Deb.PSPBadges.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
var wasLeftPrice;var nowLeftPrice;
var currentPrice;var originalPrice;

$Deb.isFurniturePSP = false;

function isPSPBadgePage(){
    if($('body').attr('id')!='WC_Shop_ProductSelectionPage_PSP_Body') return 0;
    if(location.href.indexOf('&searchKeywords=')>=0) return 0;
    var c=$('#breadcrumb_cat .breadcrumb').map( function( i, el ){ return $(el).text(); });
    if(c.length>1){
        for (var i=0; i<c.length; i++){
            var fragment=$.trim(c[i]);
           if(fragment=='Duty free') return 0;
			if(fragment=='Furniture'){
				$Deb.isFurniturePSP = true;
				return 1;
			}
        }
    }else return 1;
return 1;
};
//Standard Inject PSP badges
function inject_PSP_badges(){

	$Deb.disabledDiscountBadges = "|chanel|mac cosmetics|";

	var selectors = {
		"psp": { //Standard PSPs
			"divItems": "#gird_view .item, #four-grid .item",
			"productDivs": '[id^="psp_"]',
			"idReplace" : "psp_",
			"priceNow": ".price_now",
			"priceWas": ".listprice-01",
			"brandname": ".brand_name"
		},
		"cpl": { //Composite Pick Lists
			"divItems" : "#product_results .product_detail",
			"productDivs" : 'a[id^="img"]',
			"idReplace" : "img",
			"priceNow" : ".product_price.latest",
			"priceWas" : ".product_price:not(.latest)",
			"brandname": ".brand_name"
		},
		"rsp": { //Range selection
			"divItems" : "#productDisplay .item",
			"productDivs" : 'h3'
		}
	};

	var jSel = selectors["psp"];

	if ($(selectors["cpl"]["divItems"]).length){
		jSel = selectors["cpl"];
		$Deb.isCompositePickList = true;
	}
	
	// RSP
	if ($('body').hasClass('rsp')){
		jSel = selectors["rsp"];
		$Deb.isRangeSelectionPage = true;
	}
	
	var $productDivItems = $(jSel["divItems"]);
	var $productDivs = $productDivItems.find(jSel["productDivs"]);
	
	$Deb.productIDs = [];
	
	if (! $Deb.isRangeSelectionPage) {
		for(var i=0, len = $productDivs.length; i < len; i++){
			$Deb.productIDs.push($productDivs[i].id.replace(jSel["idReplace"],""));
		}	
	}
	
	var normalisePricesTextRegex = new RegExp(',', 'g');

	
	// Run RSP code first
	if ($Deb.isRangeSelectionPage) {
		
		//RSPs use product names
		$Deb.rspProductNames = [];
		for(var i=0, len = $productDivs.length; i < len; i++){
			$Deb.rspProductNames.push( $($productDivs[i]).text().toLowerCase() );
		}
		
		$productDivItems.each(function(idx){
			
			var badgeApplied = false;
			
			if (typeof $Deb.RSPBadgeGroups !== 'undefined') {			
				var i = 0;
				
				while(!badgeApplied && i < $Deb.RSPBadgeGroups.length) {
					var rspBadgeGroupName = ($Deb.RSPBadgeGroups[i].list).toLowerCase();
					
					if(rspBadgeGroupName.indexOf( '|' + $Deb.rspProductNames[idx] + '|') >= 0){
						$(this).find('.range').after('<div class="productTxtCls"><span class="discount_price"><span style="font-weight:bold;">'+$Deb.RSPBadgeGroups[i].message+'</span></span></div>');
						badgeApplied = true;
					}
					i++;
				};				
			}
		});
		return;
	}
	
	//The standard Product Badge Code
	$productDivItems.each(function(idx){
		var badgeApplied = false;
		
		if (typeof $Deb.badgeGroups !== 'undefined') {			
			var i = 0;
			while(!badgeApplied && (i < $Deb.badgeGroups.length)) {
				if($Deb.badgeGroups[i].list.indexOf( '|' + $Deb.productIDs[idx] + '|') >= 0){
				$(this).find('.price').parent().append('<span class="quickDelivery_badge" style="border-color:'+$Deb.badgeGroups[i].colour+';color:'+$Deb.badgeGroups[i].colour+';"><span style="border-color:'+$Deb.badgeGroups[i].colour+';color:'+$Deb.badgeGroups[i].colour+';">'+$Deb.badgeGroups[i].message+'</span></span>');					badgeApplied = true;

				}
				i++;
			}				
		}

		
		//Check if brand is disabled
		var productBrand = "|" + $.trim($(this).find(jSel["brandname"]).text().toLowerCase()) + "|";
		var disabledBadge = $Deb.disabledDiscountBadges.indexOf(productBrand) > -1;

		if (!disabledBadge && $(jSel["priceNow"],this).length){
			var wasPriceDivTxt=$.trim($(jSel["priceWas"],this).eq(0).text().replace(normalisePricesTextRegex,''));
			var nowPriceDivTxt=$.trim($(jSel["priceNow"],this).eq(0).text().replace(normalisePricesTextRegex,''));
			var isRange=(wasPriceDivTxt+''+nowPriceDivTxt).indexOf("-");
			var currencySymbol = String.fromCharCode(163);
			wasLeftPrice=parseFloat(wasPriceDivTxt.substring(wasPriceDivTxt.indexOf(currencySymbol)+1));
			nowLeftPrice=parseFloat(nowPriceDivTxt.substring(nowPriceDivTxt.indexOf(currencySymbol)+1));
			wasRightPrice=parseFloat(wasPriceDivTxt.substring(wasPriceDivTxt.lastIndexOf(currencySymbol)+1));
			nowRightPrice=parseFloat(nowPriceDivTxt.substring(nowPriceDivTxt.lastIndexOf(currencySymbol)+1));
			var leftSavingPercent=Math.floor(100 * (wasLeftPrice-nowLeftPrice)/wasLeftPrice+0.005);
			var rightSavingPercent=Math.floor(100 * (wasRightPrice-nowRightPrice)/wasRightPrice+0.005);
			var maxSavingPercents = Math.max(rightSavingPercent,leftSavingPercent);
			var discount_string=(isRange!='-1') ? 'UP TO '+maxSavingPercents+'% OFF' : 'SAVE '+maxSavingPercents+'%'
			if(maxSavingPercents>0){$(this).find('.price').prepend('<div class="productTxtCls"><span class="discount_price"><span>'+discount_string+'</span></span></div>');}
		}
		
	});
};

if(isPSPBadgePage()){inject_PSP_badges();}
</script>

/* fix beauty sub-tcats adspot link colour - force black */
if( $('body').attr('id')=='WC_Shop_TopCategory_TCAT_Body' ){

	if(c.length>1 && $.trim(c[c.length-1])=='Beauty'){
		$('#espotalign_cat .advert_third a span').css('color','#000');
	}

<script src="/wcsstore/DebenhamsStorefrontAssetStore/javascript/jquery.simplemodal.js"></script>
<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
	var $modalLink = $('.deb-sm-link');
	if(!$modalLink.length)return;
	$modalLink.bind('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		var popupImg = $(this).attr('data-popup-img'),
			popupTcLink = $(this).attr('data-popup-tc'),
			modalData = '';
		if (typeof popupTcLink !== 'undefined') {
			modalData = '<a class="tandc" href="javascript:var tmp=window.open(\''+ popupTcLink +'\',\'\',\'height=606,width=1020,scrollbars=yes,resizable=1\',toolbar=\'no\');"></a>';
		} 
		$.modal(modalData, {
			zIndex:9000,
			overlayId:"SM-overlay",
			containerId:"SM-dialog",
			containerCss:{backgroundImage : 'url(' + popupImg + ')'},
			overlayCss:{backgroundColor: '#000'},
			onShow:function(){
				$(window).resize();
			}
		});
	});
});
</script>

<script>
(function () {
	if ($Deb.isPDP) {
		// expand and collapse
		//------------------------------------------------------
		var $viewMore = $('.deb-vmore');
		$viewMore.addClass('collapsed');
		$viewMore.find('> a').click(function (e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			var $wrapper = $(this).parent();
			$wrapper.toggleClass('expanded');
			$wrapper.find('.collapsed-content').slideToggle('fast');
		});

		// Remove was price PDPs
		//------------------------------------------------------
		var brand = $('meta[property="brand"]').attr('content').toLowerCase();
		if (brand == 'mac cosmetics') {
			var $prices = $('.prices');				
			if ( $prices.find('span').hasClass('price-was') ) {
				var $nowPrice = $prices.find('.price-is');
				$prices.find('.price-was, .now1, .price-off-and-save').remove();
				$nowPrice.text($nowPrice.text().replace('Now', ''));
					// hide dynamic discount price
					$prices.append('<style>#add-to-bag-block #selected_pricing .off,#add-to-bag-block #selected_pricing .save{display:none;}</style>');
			}
		}
	}
})();
</script>

<script>
// Flix Media Product Tour Button - only needed on PDPs
if ($Deb.isPDP){
// needs to happen after the pdp.js code which builds the viewer controls
$(document).ready(function(){
	$('#info1').find('li:contains("EAN:")').each(function(){
		var EAN = $.trim($(this).text().replace('EAN:',''));
		
		if(EAN){
			// inject the flix container div
			$('#pdp-controls').prepend('<div id="flix-minisite" style="position: relative;padding-right: 65px;padding-bottom: 5px;text-align: right;"></div>');
			// new script element
			var fm = document.createElement('script');
			fm.type='text/javascript';
			fm.async=true;
			fm.src='http://media.flixfacts.com/js/loader.js';
			// product-specific
			fm.setAttribute('data-flix-ean',EAN);
			fm.setAttribute('data-flix-brand',tagData.product.brand);
			// constant
			fm.setAttribute('data-flix-distributor','5972');
			fm.setAttribute('data-flix-language','en');
			fm.setAttribute('data-flix-button','flix-minisite');
			fm.setAttribute('data-flix-button-image','/wcsstore/DebenhamsStorefrontAssetStore/img/pdp-product-tour-2.png');
			// inject the script element
			var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
			s.parentNode.insertBefore(fm, s);
		}
	});
});
}
</script>
